ldmc_pslv.ldc_referenceid) r_ldmc LEFT JOIN (SELECT leafspecificmethodid AS lfm_id, leafspecificmethodname AS lfm_name FROM (select leafspecificmethodid, leafspecificmethodname from leafspecificmethod_lv)) lfm ON r_ldmc.ldc_specificmethodid = lfm.lfm_id) ldmc_lfm ON m.m_methodid = ldmc_lfm.ldc_methodid) m_ldmc ON sbs.sbs_sbsnumber = m_ldmc.ldc_sbsnumber)) ORDER BY sbs_sbsname"
